# Comprehensive Gameplay Variable Audit

Generated by static inspection of the project’s Dry scene/state files, qdisplay files, and source configuration files. The game stores most gameplay values as Dry qualities (`Q.<name>` in script blocks or bare quality names in scene directives). Dynamic `Q[...]` families used by election and post-event logic are expanded explicitly below.

## Methodology

- Scanned `source/**/*.dry`, qdisplay files, source script blocks, and project JSON/TypeScript candidates for direct `Q.<variable>` references, bare Dry quality references, assignments, and dynamic `Q[...]` patterns. No TypeScript gameplay files and no gameplay JSON files are present in this repository; `package.json` contains package metadata only.
- Treated `source/scenes/root.scene.dry` initial assignments as primary definitions when present. Otherwise, the earliest write site is listed as the definition.
- `Modified` lists write sites and normalization/update sites; `Read/used` lists non-write usage and display/condition sites. Large repeated dynamic families list the generating files/lines rather than every runtime key expansion.

## High-level findings

- Total gameplay/state variables and expanded dynamic qualities identified: **1046**.
- **Economy:** 45 variables.
- **Culture/demographics:** 41 variables.
- **Party support/elections:** 339 variables.
- **Factions/party unity:** 30 variables.
- **Coalitions/ministries:** 67 variables.
- **Foreign relations:** 27 variables.
- **Presidency/elections:** 119 variables.
- **Security/regional/extremism:** 76 variables.
- **Hidden trackers/flags:** 102 variables.
- **Core/time/UI/timers:** 65 variables.
- **Other gameplay state:** 135 variables.

### Duplicate or overlapping variables

- **`electoral_threshold`:** Initialized twice in `root.scene.dry`; both writes set the same baseline and should be consolidated.
- **`dissent` / `dissent_percent`:** `dissent` is the fractional gameplay value; `dissent_percent` is display-oriented and can drift unless always recomputed.
- **`*_votes`, `*_votes_dec`, `*_votes_disp`, `*_votes_display`:** Election display values overlap; some paths use `_disp`, others `_display`.
- **`*_r`, `*_r_disp`, `old_*_r`, `change_*_r`, `str_change_*`:** Reichstag result, display, old result, numeric change, and string change are separate qualities for the same election result family.
- **`spd_in_government` and `in_*_coalition` flags:** Government membership and coalition-type flags overlap and must be kept synchronized after elections.
- **`minority_government` and `in_minority_government`:** One describes presidential-minority government status while the other marks SPD minority-government participation; naming is easy to confuse.
- **`wtb_support`, `wtb_adopted`, `economic_plan`, `works_program`, `wtb_implemented`:** Multiple layers represent support, adoption, plan type, implementation progress, and completion for work-creation policy.
- **`nationalization_support`, `nationalization_adopted`, `nationalization_progress`, `nationalize_budget`:** Multiple variables track related nationalization policy state.

### Unused, partially implemented, or fragile variables

- **`use_decimals`:** Commented as TODO/not yet implemented; election paths check it but default remains disabled.
- **`workers_qol`, `rural_qol`, `unemployed_qol`, `old_middle_qol`, `new_middle_qol`:** Comment says quality of life is currently unused and should be welfare-adjusted.
- **`old_demographics`:** Switch exists in election calculations but appears to be a compatibility/alternate algorithm flag rather than active design surface.
- **`national unity government`:** Root comment notes it, and `in_unity_government` is assigned dynamically after elections, but it lacks the same root initialization block/commenting as other coalition flags.
- **Dynamic party families for `sapd`:** `sapd` is not in the initial `parties` array, but many dynamic expansions need SAPD support once formed; audit includes it as a runtime family.
- **`*_goal` / `*_goal_completed` families:** Coalition/ministry goals are created after elections; they are partially documented in election code rather than initialized with the rest of government state.
- **`mods_table`:** Created by mod-loader code and not part of initial root state; save/load expectations should be verified if mods are gameplay-relevant.

### Systems that probably need additional variables

- **Regional/federal politics:** Only Prussia has deep state; additional Länder variables would support federal politics beyond `spd_prussia`/`prussian_government`.
- **Culture policy outcomes:** Culture/civil-rights variables exist, but persistent backlash/support-by-demographic trackers could make reforms less one-dimensional.
- **Foreign relations granularity:** West/east/Soviet relations are broad; separate France/UK/Poland/Czechoslovakia/Austria variables may help event specificity.
- **Institutional legitimacy:** `pro_republic` is broad; separate court, bureaucracy, army, presidential, and Reichstag legitimacy could reduce overload.
- **Coalition promises:** Goal variables exist by ministry, but coalition-agreement severity/deadline/owner variables would make failures easier to reason about.
- **Extremist violence:** Militancy and strength exist by organization, but separate incident frequency, casualties, public fear, and policing legitimacy could enrich street politics.

## Engine/runtime state fields

These are Dendry engine/UI state fields rather than gameplay qualities, but they affect save/load, card flow, scene navigation, or display.

| State field | Defined/modified | Read/used | Purpose |
|---|---|---|---|
| `state.qualities` | — | `out/html/game.js:193,246` | Container for Dry qualities (`Q.*`), including checks such as disabling polls in historical mode. |
| `state.sceneId` | — | `out/html/game.js:29,38,174` | Current scene identifier used by UI/library/mod-loader behavior. |
| `state.bg` | — | `out/html/game.js:73` | Current background image consumed by the UI. |
| `state.currentHands` | `source/scenes/advisors/wels.scene.dry:26,28`; `source/scenes/easy_discard.scene.dry:12,14` | `source/scenes/advisors/wels.scene.dry:26,28`; `source/scenes/easy_discard.scene.dry:12,14` | Card-hand storage for main/easy decks; manipulated when cards are returned or hands cleared. |
| `state.disableSaves` | `source/scenes/root.scene.dry:619` | — | Save-disable flag set by historical mode. |
| `state.prevTopSceneId` | — | `source/scenes/cancel_advisor_action.scene.dry:16` | Previous scene/card id used when canceling advisor/cabinet actions. |
| `state.lastPlayedCard` | — | `source/scenes/easy_discard.scene.dry:9` | Last card object used for easy-discard card-return logic. |
| `state.visits` | `source/scenes/cancel_advisor_action.scene.dry:22`; `source/scenes/easy_discard.scene.dry:22` | `source/scenes/cancel_advisor_action.scene.dry:21`; `source/scenes/easy_discard.scene.dry:21` | Visit counts decremented when canceled/discarded cards should not count as consumed. |
